	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php') != '542bacd5a920dc23b5d5c36fd8b71a12f3b2ae02') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php') !== '542bacd5a920dc23b5d5c36fd8b71a12f3b2ae02') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php') !== '26e238544a8d2a485e7f026872dd81d4455249be') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php') !== '542bacd5a920dc23b5d5c36fd8b71a12f3b2ae02') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/path-converter/Converter.php');
		}
	}

	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') != '84c63c566732da275007c8aa112d614df2a92630') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/src/CSS.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') !== '84c63c566732da275007c8aa112d614df2a92630') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') !== '42687ac29102960a3a88f5304a4f4031d250069f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/minify/src/CSS.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/src/CSS.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') !== '84c63c566732da275007c8aa112d614df2a92630') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') != '4b022053cf061e6aee001c3782e20670cee687c3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/src/JS.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') !== '4b022053cf061e6aee001c3782e20670cee687c3') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') !== '3b0c298c1b5ae0c3f6cb91ba152544ad5053c5be') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/minify/src/JS.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/minify/src/JS.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/src/JS.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') !== '4b022053cf061e6aee001c3782e20670cee687c3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') != 'f14e31062cad98dec1668f7e9524411efee3b6a1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/src/Minify.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') !== 'f14e31062cad98dec1668f7e9524411efee3b6a1') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') !== 'd6041e193c5b6208503ac7f76f69ab93e4263992') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/minify/src/Minify.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/src/Minify.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') !== 'f14e31062cad98dec1668f7e9524411efee3b6a1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
		}
	}
}
